##  Addons Tweaks

### ElvUI

#### Add Fonts

`Interface\AddOns\ElvUI\Media`

1. Copy file to `Interface\AddOns\ElvUI\Media\Fonts\YouyuanHeiti.ttf`.
2. Edit `SharedMedia.lua`.

```lua
E.Media = {
	Fonts = {YouyuanHeiti = M..[[Fonts\YouyuanHeiti.ttf]]}
}

LSM:Register("font", "Youyuan Heiti", E.Media.Fonts.YouyuanHeiti)
```

#### Action Bar Paging

`WTF\Account\ABSTRACTACCOUNT\SavedVariables\ElvUI.lua\ElvDB.profiles.zhengyuan.actionbar.bar1`

```lua
["paging"] = {
	["DRUID"] = "[stance:0/2/3/4/5/6]1; [stance:1]10;",
	["WARRIOR"] = "[stance:1/2/3]1;",
	["ROGUE"] = "[stance:1/2]10;",
}
```

Druid

| Stance Number |                                     |
| :-----------: | :---------------------------------: |
|       0       |               Caster                |
|       1       |                Bear                 |
|       2       |               Aquatic               |
|       3       |                 Cat                 |
|       4       |              Traveler               |
|       5       |  Moonkin/Tree of Life/Flight  |
|       *6       | Flight (If no stance 5) |

Warrior

| Stance Number |              |
| :-----------: | :----------: |
|       1       |    Battle Stance    |
|       2       |   Defensive Stance    |
|       3       | Berserker stance |

Rogue

| Stance Number |              |
| :-----------: | :----------: |
|       0       |    Caster    |
|       1       |   Stealth    |
|       2       | Shadow Dance |

#### Top/Bottom Panel

`ElvUI/Layout/Layout.lua`

```lua
local PANEL_HEIGHT = 22

function LO:Initialize()
    self.BottomPanel:Height(PANEL_HEIGHT)
    self.TopPanel:Height(PANEL_HEIGHT)
end
```
